Shader "Hidden/Internal-PrePassCollectShadows" {
Properties {
 _ShadowMapTexture ("", any) = "" { }
}
SubShader { 
 Pass {
  ZTest Always
  ZWrite Off
  Cull Off
  GpuProgramID 58189
Program "vp" {
SubProgram "gles " {
Keywords { "SHADOWS_NONATIVE" }
"!!GLES
#version 100

#ifdef VERTEX
attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
uniform highp vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform highp mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD2;
void main ()
{
  highp vec4 clipPos_1;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_2;
  tmpvar_2 = (glstate_matrix_mvp * _glesVertex);
  clipPos_1.xzw = tmpvar_2.xzw;
  clipPos_1.y = (tmpvar_2.y * _ProjectionParams.x);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_3;
  tmpvar_3.zw = vec2(-1.0, 1.0);
  tmpvar_3.xy = clipPos_1.xy;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4 = (unity_CameraInvProjection * tmpvar_3);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5.zw = vec2(1.0, 1.0);
  tmpvar_5.xy = clipPos_1.xy;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6.xy = tmpvar_4.xy;
  tmpvar_6.z = -(tmpvar_4.z);
  tmpvar_6.w = -((unity_CameraInvProjection * tmpvar_5).z);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = _glesMultiTexCoord0.xy;
  xlv_TEXCOORD1 = _glesNormal;
  xlv_TEXCOORD2 = tmpvar_6;
  gl_Position = tmpvar_2;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
uniform highp vec4 _ZBufferParams;
uniform highp vec4 unity_OrthoParams;
uniform highp vec4 _LightSplitsNear;
uniform highp vec4 _LightSplitsFar;
uniform highp mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform highp sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform highp mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD2;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 res_1;
  mediump float shadow_2;
  highp vec3 vposOrtho_3;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4 = texture2D (_CameraDepthTexture, xlv_TEXCOORD0);
  vposOrtho_3.xy = xlv_TEXCOORD2.xy;
  vposOrtho_3.z = mix (xlv_TEXCOORD2.z, xlv_TEXCOORD2.w, tmpvar_4.x);
  highp vec3 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5 = mix ((xlv_TEXCOORD1 * mix (
    (1.0/(((_ZBufferParams.x * tmpvar_4.x) + _ZBufferParams.y)))
  , tmpvar_4.x, unity_OrthoParams.w)), vposOrtho_3, unity_OrthoParams.www);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_6.xyz = tmpvar_5;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_7;
  tmpvar_7 = (_CameraToWorld * tmpvar_6);
  bvec4 tmpvar_8;
  tmpvar_8 = greaterThanEqual (tmpvar_5.zzzz, _LightSplitsNear);
  bvec4 tmpvar_9;
  tmpvar_9 = lessThan (tmpvar_5.zzzz, _LightSplitsFar);
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_10;
  tmpvar_10 = (vec4(tmpvar_8) * vec4(tmpvar_9));
  highp vec4 tmpvar_11;
  tmpvar_11.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_11.xyz = (((
    ((unity_World2Shadow[0] * tmpvar_7).xyz * tmpvar_10.x)
   + 
    ((unity_World2Shadow[1] * tmpvar_7).xyz * tmpvar_10.y)
  ) + (
    (unity_World2Shadow[2] * tmpvar_7)
  .xyz * tmpvar_10.z)) + ((unity_World2Shadow[3] * tmpvar_7).xyz * tmpvar_10.w));
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_12;
  tmpvar_12 = texture2D (_ShadowMapTexture, tmpvar_11.xy);
  mediump float tmpvar_13;
  if ((tmpvar_12.x < tmpvar_11.z)) {
    tmpvar_13 = 0.0;
  } else {
    tmpvar_13 = 1.0;
  };
  highp float tmpvar_14;
  tmpvar_14 = clamp (((tmpvar_5.z * _LightShadowData.z) + _LightShadowData.w), 0.0, 1.0);
  shadow_2 = (mix (_LightShadowData.x, 1.0, tmpvar_13) + tmpvar_14);
  mediump vec4 tmpvar_15;
  tmpvar_15 = vec4(shadow_2);
  res_1 = tmpvar_15;
  gl_FragData[0] = res_1;
}


#endif
"
}

Keywords { "SHADOWS_NATIVE" }
"!!GLSL#version 120

#ifdef VERTEX
uniform vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;

varying vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
varying vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD2;

  vec4 clipPos_1;

  xlv_TEXCOORD1 = gl_Normal;
  xlv_TEXCOORD2 = tmpvar_6;
  gl_Position = tmpvar_2;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

uniform vec4 unity_OrthoParams;

uniform vec4 _LightSplitsFar;

void main ()
{
  vec3 vposOrtho_1;
  vec4 tmpvar_2;
  tmpvar_2 = texture2D (_CameraDepthTexture, xlv_TEXCOORD0);
  vposOrtho_1.xy = xlv_TEXCOORD2.xy;
  vposOrtho_1.z = mix (xlv_TEXCOORD2.z, xlv_TEXCOORD2.w, tmpvar_2.x);
  vec3 tmpvar_3;
  tmpvar_3 = mix ((xlv_TEXCOORD1 * mix (
    (1.0/(((_ZBufferParams.x * tmpvar_2.x) + _ZBufferParams.y)))
  , tmpvar_2.x, unity_OrthoParams.w)), vposOrtho_1, unity_OrthoParams.www);
  vec4 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_4.xyz = tmpvar_3;
  vec4 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5 = (_CameraToWorld * tmpvar_4);
  vec4 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6 = (vec4(greaterThanEqual (tmpvar_3.zzzz, _LightSplitsNear)) * vec4(lessThan (tmpvar_3.zzzz, _LightSplitsFar)));
  vec4 tmpvar_7;
  tmpvar_7.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_7.xyz = (((
    ((unity_World2Shadow[0] * tmpvar_5).xyz * tmpvar_6.x)
   + 
    ((unity_World2Shadow[1] * tmpvar_5).xyz * tmpvar_6.y)
  ) + (
    (unity_World2Shadow[2] * tmpvar_5)
  .xyz * tmpvar_6.z)) + ((unity_World2Shadow[3] * tmpvar_5).xyz * tmpvar_6.w));
  gl_FragData[0] = vec4((mix (_LightShadowData.x, 1.0, shadow2D (_ShadowMapTexture, tmpvar_7.xyz).x) + clamp ((
    (tmpvar_3.z * _LightShadowData.z)
   + _LightShadowData.w), 0.0, 1.0)));
}


#endif
"

dcl_texcoord v1
dcl_normal v2

mov r1.zw, c8.xyxy
dp4 r1.x, c0, v0
dp4 oT2.x, c4, r1
dp4 oT2.y, c5, r1
dp4 r0.x, c6, r1
dp4 r0.y, c6, r1.xyww

mov oT2.zw, -r0.xyxy
mov oT0.xy, v1
mov oT1.xyz, v2

uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec3 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 126
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 127
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 128
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 129
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 130
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 131
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 132
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 133
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 134
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 135
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 136
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 137
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 138
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 139
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = vec3(t0.y * float(1.0), t0.z * float(1.0), t0.w * float(-1.0));
    //Instruction 140
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 141
    //RET
    return;
}

#version 300 es
precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 _SinTime;
uniform 	vec4 _CosTime;

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _ProjectionParams;

uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraProjection;
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;
uniform 	vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;
uniform 	vec4 _LightPositionRange;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosX0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosY0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosZ0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_4LightAtten0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightColor[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightPosition[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightAtten[8];

uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor0;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor1;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor2;

uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[4];

uniform 	vec4 unity_LightShadowBias;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsNear;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsFar;
uniform 	mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;

uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;

uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;

uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;

uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;

uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
uniform highp sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
lowp vec4 t10_1;
bvec4 tb1;
highp vec4 t2;
bvec4 tb2;
highp vec3 t3;
mediump float t16_4;
highp vec3 t5;
lowp float t10_5;
highp float t10;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 79
    //SAMPLE
    t0.x = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    //Instruction 80
    //MAD
    t5.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 81
    //DIV
    t5.x = float(1.0) / t5.x;
    //Instruction 82
    //ADD
    t10 = (-t5.x) + t0.x;
    //Instruction 83
    //MAD
    t5.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t10 + t5.x;
    //Instruction 84
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 85
    //ADD
    t10 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 86
    //MAD
    t1.z = t0.x * t10 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 87
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t5.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 88
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t5.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 89
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 90
    //GE
    tb1 = greaterThanEqual(t0.zzzz, _LightSplitsNear);
    //Instruction 91
    //AND
    t1 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb1);
    //Instruction 92
    //LT
    tb2 = lessThan(t0.zzzz, _LightSplitsFar);
    //Instruction 93
    //AND
    t2 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb2);
    //Instruction 94
    //MUL
    t10_1 = t1 * t2;
    //Instruction 95
    //MUL
    t2 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 96
    //MAD
    t2 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t2;
    //Instruction 97
    //MAD
    t2 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t2;
    //Instruction 98
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.z * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 99
    //ADD
    t2 = t2 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 100
    //MUL
    t5.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[1][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 101
    //MAD
    t5.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 102
    //MAD
    t5.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 103
    //MAD
    t5.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][3].xyz * t2.www + t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 104
    //MUL
    t5.xyz = t10_1.yyy * t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 105
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 106
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 107
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 108
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t2.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 109
    //MAD
    t5.xyz = t3.xyz * t10_1.xxx + t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 110
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[2][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 111
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 112
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 113
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][3].xyz * t2.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 114
    //MAD
    t5.xyz = t3.xyz * t10_1.zzz + t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 115
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[3][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 116
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 117
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 118
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][3].xyz * t2.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 119
    //MAD
    t5.xyz = t2.xyz * t10_1.www + t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 120
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(t5.xy,t5.z);
    t10_5 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    //Instruction 121
    //ADD
    t16_4 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 122
    //MAD
    t16_4 = t10_5 * t16_4 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 123
    //ADD
    t0 = t0.xxxx + vec4(t16_4);
    //Instruction 124
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 125
    //RET
    return;
}

void main()
{
    //Instruction 247
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 248
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 249
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 250
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 251
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 252
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 253
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 254
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 255
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 256
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 257

    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 258
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 259
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 260
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = t0.yzw * vec3(1.0, 1.0, -1.0);
    //Instruction 261
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 262
    //RET
    return;

uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	vec4 unity_AmbientSky;

uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;

uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
uniform  sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform  sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform  sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in  vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in  vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in  vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 t0;
lowp vec4 t10_0;
vec4 t1;
bvec4 tb1;
vec4 t2;
bvec4 tb2;
vec3 t3;
vec3 t4;
lowp float t10_4;
float t8;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 201
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    //Instruction 202
    //MAD
    t4.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t10_0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 203
    //DIV
    t4.x = float(1.0) / t4.x;
    //Instruction 204
    //ADD
    t8 = (-t4.x) + t10_0.x;
    //Instruction 205
    //MAD
    t4.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t8 + t4.x;
    //Instruction 206
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 207
    //ADD
    t8 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 208
    //MAD
    t1.z = t10_0.x * t8 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 209
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t4.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 210
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 211
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 212
    //GE
    tb1 = greaterThanEqual(t0.zzzz, _LightSplitsNear);
    //Instruction 213
    //AND
    t1 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb1);
    //Instruction 214
    //LT
    tb2 = lessThan(t0.zzzz, _LightSplitsFar);
    //Instruction 215
    //AND
    t2 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb2);
    //Instruction 216
    //MUL
    t1 = t1 * t2;
    //Instruction 217
    //MUL
    t2 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 218
    //MAD
    t2 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t2;
    //Instruction 219
    //MAD
    t2 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t2;
    //Instruction 220
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.z * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 221
    //ADD
    t2 = t2 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 222
    //MUL
    t4.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[1][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 223
    //MAD
    t4.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t4.xyz;
    //Instruction 224
    //MAD
    t4.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t4.xyz;
    //Instruction 225
    //MAD
    t4.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][3].xyz * t2.www + t4.xyz;
    //Instruction 226
    //MUL
    t4.xyz = t1.yyy * t4.xyz;
    //Instruction 227
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 228
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 229
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 230
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t2.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 231
    //MAD
    t4.xyz = t3.xyz * t1.xxx + t4.xyz;
    //Instruction 232
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[2][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 233
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 234
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 235
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][3].xyz * t2.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 236
    //MAD
    t4.xyz = t3.xyz * t1.zzz + t4.xyz;
    //Instruction 237
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[3][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 238
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 239
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 240
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][3].xyz * t2.www + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 241
    //MAD
    t4.xyz = t1.xyz * t1.www + t4.xyz;
    //Instruction 242
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(t4.xy,t4.z);
    t10_4 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    //Instruction 243
    //ADD
    t8 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 244
    //MAD
    t4.x = t10_4 * t8 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 245
    //ADD
    SV_Target0 = t0.xxxx + t4.xxxx;
    //Instruction 246
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
SubProgram "gles " {
Keywords { "SHADOWS_SPLIT_SPHERES" "SHADOWS_NONATIVE" }
"!!GLES
#version 100

#ifdef FRAGMENT

uniform highp mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD2;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 res_1;
  mediump float shadow_2;
  highp vec3 vposOrtho_3;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4 = texture2D (_CameraDepthTexture, xlv_TEXCOORD0);
  vposOrtho_3.xy = xlv_TEXCOORD2.xy;
  vposOrtho_3.z = mix (xlv_TEXCOORD2.z, xlv_TEXCOORD2.w, tmpvar_4.x);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_5.xyz = mix ((xlv_TEXCOORD1 * mix (
    (1.0/(((_ZBufferParams.x * tmpvar_4.x) + _ZBufferParams.y)))
  , tmpvar_4.x, unity_OrthoParams.w)), vposOrtho_3, unity_OrthoParams.www);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6 = (_CameraToWorld * tmpvar_5);
  lowp vec4 weights_7;

  tmpvar_8 = (tmpvar_6.xyz - unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[0].xyz);
  highp vec3 tmpvar_9;
  tmpvar_9 = (tmpvar_6.xyz - unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[1].xyz);
  highp vec3 tmpvar_10;
  tmpvar_10 = (tmpvar_6.xyz - unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[2].xyz);
  highp vec3 tmpvar_11;
  tmpvar_11 = (tmpvar_6.xyz - unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[3].xyz);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_12;
  tmpvar_12.x = dot (tmpvar_8, tmpvar_8);
  tmpvar_12.y = dot (tmpvar_9, tmpvar_9);
  tmpvar_12.z = dot (tmpvar_10, tmpvar_10);
  tmpvar_12.w = dot (tmpvar_11, tmpvar_11);
  bvec4 tmpvar_13;
  tmpvar_13 = lessThan (tmpvar_12, unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii);
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_14;
  tmpvar_14 = vec4(tmpvar_13);
  weights_7.x = tmpvar_14.x;
  weights_7.yzw = clamp ((tmpvar_14.yzw - tmpvar_14.xyz), 0.0, 1.0);

  tmpvar_15.w = 1.0;

    ((unity_World2Shadow[0] * tmpvar_6).xyz * tmpvar_14.x)
   + 
    ((unity_World2Shadow[1] * tmpvar_6).xyz * weights_7.y)
  ) + (
    (unity_World2Shadow[2] * tmpvar_6)
  .xyz * weights_7.z)) + ((unity_World2Shadow[3] * tmpvar_6).xyz * weights_7.w));
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_16;
  tmpvar_16 = texture2D (_ShadowMapTexture, tmpvar_15.xy);
  mediump float tmpvar_17;
  if ((tmpvar_16.x < tmpvar_15.z)) {
    tmpvar_17 = 0.0;
  } else {
    tmpvar_17 = 1.0;
  };
  highp float tmpvar_18;
  highp vec3 tmpvar_19;
  tmpvar_19 = (tmpvar_6.xyz - unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
  mediump float tmpvar_20;
  highp float tmpvar_21;

    sqrt(dot (tmpvar_19, tmpvar_19))
   * _LightShadowData.z) + _LightShadowData.w), 0.0, 1.0);

  tmpvar_18 = tmpvar_20;

SubProgram "gles3 " {
Keywords { "SHADOWS_SPLIT_SPHERES" "SHADOWS_NATIVE" }
"!!GLES3
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 300 es
precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 _SinTime;
uniform 	vec4 _CosTime;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DeltaTime;
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ScreenParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ZBufferParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_OrthoParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_CameraWorldClipPlanes[6];
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraProjection;
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;
uniform 	vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;
uniform 	vec4 _LightPositionRange;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosX0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosY0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosZ0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_4LightAtten0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightColor[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightPosition[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightAtten[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpotDirection[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor0;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor1;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor2;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor3;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[4];
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightShadowBias;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsNear;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsFar;
uniform 	mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;
uniform 	mat4 _World2Object;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_transpose_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;
uniform 	lowp vec4 glstate_lightmodel_ambient;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientGround;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec3 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 200
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 201
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 202
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 203
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 204
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 205
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 206
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 207
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 208
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 209
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 210
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 211
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 212
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 213
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = vec3(t0.y * float(1.0), t0.z * float(1.0), t0.w * float(-1.0));
    //Instruction 214
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 215
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es
precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 _SinTime;
uniform 	vec4 _CosTime;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DeltaTime;
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ScreenParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ZBufferParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_OrthoParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_CameraWorldClipPlanes[6];
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraProjection;
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;
uniform 	vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;
uniform 	vec4 _LightPositionRange;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosX0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosY0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosZ0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_4LightAtten0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightColor[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightPosition[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightAtten[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpotDirection[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor0;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor1;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor2;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor3;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[4];
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightShadowBias;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsNear;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsFar;
uniform 	mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;
uniform 	mat4 _World2Object;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_transpose_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;
uniform 	lowp vec4 glstate_lightmodel_ambient;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientGround;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
uniform highp sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
bvec4 tb1;
highp vec3 t2;
lowp vec3 t10_3;
mediump float t16_4;
highp vec3 t5;
lowp float t10_5;
highp vec3 t6;
highp float t10;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 142
    //SAMPLE
    t0.x = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    //Instruction 143
    //MAD
    t5.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 144
    //DIV
    t5.x = float(1.0) / t5.x;
    //Instruction 145
    //ADD
    t10 = (-t5.x) + t0.x;
    //Instruction 146
    //MAD
    t5.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t10 + t5.x;
    //Instruction 147
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 148
    //ADD
    t10 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 149
    //MAD
    t1.z = t0.x * t10 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 150
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t5.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 151
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t5.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 152
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 153
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 154
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 155
    //MAD
    t0 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 156
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 157
    //ADD
    t1.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[0].xyz);
    //Instruction 158
    //DP3
    t1.x = dot(t1.xyz, t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 159
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[1].xyz);
    //Instruction 160
    //DP3
    t1.y = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 161
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 162
    //DP3
    t1.z = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 163
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[3].xyz);
    //Instruction 164
    //DP3
    t1.w = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 165
    //LT
    tb1 = lessThan(t1, unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii);
    //Instruction 166
    //MOVC
    t10_3.x = (tb1.x) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    t10_3.y = (tb1.y) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    t10_3.z = (tb1.z) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    //Instruction 167
    //AND
    t1 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb1);
    //Instruction 168
    //ADD
    t10_3.xyz = vec3(t10_3.x + t1.y, t10_3.y + t1.z, t10_3.z + t1.w);
    //Instruction 169
    //MAX
    t10_3.xyz = max(t10_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    //Instruction 170
    //MUL
    t6.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[1][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 171
    //MAD
    t6.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 172
    //MAD
    t6.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 173
    //MAD
    t6.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][3].xyz * t0.www + t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 174
    //MUL
    t6.xyz = t10_3.xxx * t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 175
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 176
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 177
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 178
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 179
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = t2.xyz * t1.xxx + t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 180
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[2][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 181
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 182
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 183
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 184
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = t2.xyz * t10_3.yyy + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 185
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[3][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 186
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 187
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 188
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 189
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
    //Instruction 190
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 191
    //SQRT
    t0.x = sqrt(t0.x);
    //Instruction 192
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.x * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 193
    //MAD
    t5.xyz = t2.xyz * t10_3.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 194
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(t5.xy,t5.z);
    t10_5 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    //Instruction 195
    //ADD
    t16_4 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 196
    //MAD
    t16_4 = t10_5 * t16_4 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 197
    //ADD
    t0 = t0.xxxx + vec4(t16_4);
    //Instruction 198
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 199
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
SubProgram "glcore " {
Keywords { "SHADOWS_SPLIT_SPHERES" "SHADOWS_NATIVE" }
"!!GL2x
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 150
#extension GL_ARB_shader_bit_encoding : require

uniform 	vec4 _CosTime;

uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii;

uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsFar;
uniform 	mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform 	vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;
uniform 	mat4 _World2Object;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_transpose_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;

uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;

uniform 	vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	vec4 unity_AmbientGround;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_ProbePosition;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
in  vec4 in_POSITION0;
in  vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in  vec3 in_NORMAL0;
out vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
vec4 t0;
vec3 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 96
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 97
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 98
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 99
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 100
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 101
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 102
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 103
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 104
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 105
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 106
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 107
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 108
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 109
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = t0.yzw * vec3(1.0, 1.0, -1.0);
    //Instruction 110
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 111
    //RET
    return;
}

#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 150
#extension GL_ARB_shader_bit_encoding : require
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 _SinTime;

uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
uniform  sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform  sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform  sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in  vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in  vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in  vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 t0;
lowp vec4 t10_0;
vec4 t1;
bvec4 tb1;
vec3 t2;
vec3 t3;
vec3 t4;
lowp float t10_4;
vec3 t5;
float t8;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 39
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    //Instruction 40
    //MAD
    t4.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t10_0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 41
    //DIV
    t4.x = float(1.0) / t4.x;
    //Instruction 42
    //ADD
    t8 = (-t4.x) + t10_0.x;
    //Instruction 43
    //MAD
    t4.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t8 + t4.x;
    //Instruction 44
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 45
    //ADD
    t8 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 46
    //MAD
    t1.z = t10_0.x * t8 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 47
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t4.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 48
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 49
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 50
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 51
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 52
    //MAD
    t0 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 53
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 54
    //ADD
    t1.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[0].xyz);
    //Instruction 55
    //DP3
    t1.x = dot(t1.xyz, t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 56
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[1].xyz);
    //Instruction 57
    //DP3
    t1.y = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 58
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 59
    //DP3
    t1.z = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 60
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[3].xyz);
    //Instruction 61
    //DP3
    t1.w = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 62
    //LT
    tb1 = lessThan(t1, unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii);
    //Instruction 63
    //MOVC
    t2.x = (tb1.x) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    t2.y = (tb1.y) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    t2.z = (tb1.z) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    //Instruction 64
    //AND
    t1 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb1);
    //Instruction 65
    //ADD
    t5.xyz = t2.xyz + t1.yzw;
    //Instruction 66
    //MAX
    t5.xyz = max(t5.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    //Instruction 67
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[1][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 68
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 69
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 70
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 71
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t5.xxx * t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 72
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 73
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 74
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 75
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t0.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 76
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = t3.xyz * t1.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 77
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[2][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 78
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 79
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 80
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][3].xyz * t0.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 81
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = t3.xyz * t5.yyy + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 82
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[3][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 83
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 84
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 85
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 86
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
    //Instruction 87
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 88
    //SQRT
    t0.x = sqrt(t0.x);
    //Instruction 89
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.x * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 90
    //MAD
    t4.xyz = t2.xyz * t5.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 91
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(t4.xy,t4.z);
    t10_4 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    //Instruction 92
    //ADD
    t8 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 93
    //MAD
    t4.x = t10_4 * t8 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 94
    //ADD
    SV_Target0 = t0.xxxx + t4.xxxx;
    //Instruction 95
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
SubProgram "gles " {
Keywords { "SHADOWS_SINGLE_CASCADE" "SHADOWS_NONATIVE" }
"!!GLES
#version 100

#ifdef VERTEX
attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
uniform highp vec4 _ProjectionParams;

uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD2;
void main ()
{
  highp vec4 clipPos_1;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_2;
  tmpvar_2 = (glstate_matrix_mvp * _glesVertex);
  clipPos_1.xzw = tmpvar_2.xzw;
  clipPos_1.y = (tmpvar_2.y * _ProjectionParams.x);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_3;
  tmpvar_3.zw = vec2(-1.0, 1.0);
  tmpvar_3.xy = clipPos_1.xy;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4 = (unity_CameraInvProjection * tmpvar_3);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5.zw = vec2(1.0, 1.0);
  tmpvar_5.xy = clipPos_1.xy;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6.xy = tmpvar_4.xy;
  tmpvar_6.z = -(tmpvar_4.z);
  tmpvar_6.w = -((unity_CameraInvProjection * tmpvar_5).z);
  xlv_TEXCOORD0 = _glesMultiTexCoord0.xy;
  xlv_TEXCOORD1 = _glesNormal;
  xlv_TEXCOORD2 = tmpvar_6;
  gl_Position = tmpvar_2;
}


#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
uniform highp vec4 _ZBufferParams;
uniform highp vec4 unity_OrthoParams;
uniform highp mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform highp sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform highp mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD2;
void main ()
{
  lowp vec4 res_1;
  mediump float shadow_2;
  highp vec3 vposOrtho_3;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4 = texture2D (_CameraDepthTexture, xlv_TEXCOORD0);
  vposOrtho_3.xy = xlv_TEXCOORD2.xy;
  vposOrtho_3.z = mix (xlv_TEXCOORD2.z, xlv_TEXCOORD2.w, tmpvar_4.x);
  highp vec3 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5 = mix ((xlv_TEXCOORD1 * mix (
    (1.0/(((_ZBufferParams.x * tmpvar_4.x) + _ZBufferParams.y)))
  , tmpvar_4.x, unity_OrthoParams.w)), vposOrtho_3, unity_OrthoParams.www);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_6;
  tmpvar_6.w = 1.0;
  tmpvar_6.xyz = tmpvar_5;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_7;
  tmpvar_7.w = 0.0;
  tmpvar_7.xyz = (unity_World2Shadow[0] * (_CameraToWorld * tmpvar_6)).xyz;
  lowp vec4 tmpvar_8;
  tmpvar_8 = texture2D (_ShadowMapTexture, tmpvar_7.xy);
  mediump float tmpvar_9;
  if ((tmpvar_8.x < tmpvar_7.z)) {
    tmpvar_9 = 0.0;
  } else {
    tmpvar_9 = 1.0;
  };
  highp float tmpvar_10;
  tmpvar_10 = clamp (((tmpvar_5.z * _LightShadowData.z) + _LightShadowData.w), 0.0, 1.0);
  shadow_2 = (mix (_LightShadowData.x, 1.0, tmpvar_9) + tmpvar_10);
  mediump vec4 tmpvar_11;
  tmpvar_11 = vec4(shadow_2);
  res_1 = tmpvar_11;
  gl_FragData[0] = res_1;
}


#endif
"

  tmpvar_6.xyz = tmpvar_5;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_7;
  tmpvar_7.w = 0.0;
  tmpvar_7.xyz = (unity_World2Shadow[0] * (_CameraToWorld * tmpvar_6)).xyz;
  lowp float tmpvar_8;
  tmpvar_8 = shadow2DEXT (_ShadowMapTexture, tmpvar_7.xyz);
  mediump float tmpvar_9;
  tmpvar_9 = tmpvar_8;
  highp float tmpvar_10;
  tmpvar_10 = clamp (((tmpvar_5.z * _LightShadowData.z) + _LightShadowData.w), 0.0, 1.0);
  shadow_2 = (mix (_LightShadowData.x, 1.0, tmpvar_9) + tmpvar_10);
  mediump vec4 tmpvar_11;
  tmpvar_11 = vec4(shadow_2);
  res_1 = tmpvar_11;
  gl_FragData[0] = res_1;
}


#endif
"
}

in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;

highp vec4 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
mediump float t16_2;
highp vec3 t3;
lowp float t10_3;
highp float t6;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 0
    //SAMPLE
    t0.x = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    //Instruction 1
    //MAD
    t3.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 2
    //DIV
    t3.x = float(1.0) / t3.x;
    //Instruction 3
    //ADD
    t6 = (-t3.x) + t0.x;
    //Instruction 4
    //MAD
    t3.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t6 + t3.x;
    //Instruction 5
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 6
    //ADD
    t6 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 7
    //MAD
    t1.z = t0.x * t6 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 8
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t3.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 9
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t3.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 10
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 11
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 12
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 13
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 14
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.z * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 15
    //ADD
    t1 = t1 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 16
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t1.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 17
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t1.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 18
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t1.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 19
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t1.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 20
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(t3.xy,t3.z);
    t10_3 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    //Instruction 21
    //ADD
    t16_2 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 22
    //MAD
    t16_2 = t10_3 * t16_2 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 23
    //ADD
    t0 = t0.xxxx + vec4(t16_2);
    //Instruction 24
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 25
    //RET
    return;
}

uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
uniform  sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform  sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform  sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in  vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in  vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in  vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 t0;
lowp vec4 t10_0;
vec4 t1;
vec3 t2;
lowp float t10_2;
float t4;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 84
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    //Instruction 85
    //MAD
    t2.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t10_0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 86
    //DIV
    t2.x = float(1.0) / t2.x;
    //Instruction 87
    //ADD
    t4 = (-t2.x) + t10_0.x;
    //Instruction 88
    //MAD
    t2.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t4 + t2.x;
    //Instruction 89
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 90
    //ADD
    t4 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 91
    //MAD
    t1.z = t10_0.x * t4 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 92
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t2.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 93
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 94
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 95
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 96
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 97
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 98
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.z * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 99
    //ADD
    t1 = t1 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 100
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t1.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 101
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t1.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 102
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t1.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 103
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t1.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 104
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(t2.xy,t2.z);
    t10_2 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    //Instruction 105
    //ADD
    t4 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 106
    //MAD
    t2.x = t10_2 * t4 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 107
    //ADD
    SV_Target0 = t0.xxxx + t2.xxxx;
    //Instruction 108
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"
}

SubProgram "gles3 " {
Keywords { "SHADOWS_SPLIT_SPHERES" "SHADOWS_NATIVE" "SHADOWS_SINGLE_CASCADE" }
"!!GLES3
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 300 es
precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 _SinTime;
uniform 	vec4 _CosTime;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DeltaTime;
uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ScreenParams;
uniform 	vec4 _ZBufferParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_OrthoParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_CameraWorldClipPlanes[6];
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraProjection;
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;
uniform 	vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;
uniform 	vec4 _LightPositionRange;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosX0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosY0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosZ0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_4LightAtten0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightColor[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightPosition[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightAtten[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpotDirection[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor0;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor1;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor2;
uniform 	mediump vec3 unity_LightColor3;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[4];
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightShadowBias;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsNear;
uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsFar;
uniform 	mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;
uniform 	mat4 _World2Object;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_transpose_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;
uniform 	lowp vec4 glstate_lightmodel_ambient;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientGround;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec3 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 71
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 72
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 73
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 74
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 75
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 76
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 77
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 78
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 79
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 80
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 81
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 82
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 83
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 84
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = vec3(t0.y * float(1.0), t0.z * float(1.0), t0.w * float(-1.0));
    //Instruction 85
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 86
    //RET
    return;
}

precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;

uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;
uniform 	mat4 _World2Object;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_transpose_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;
uniform 	lowp vec4 glstate_lightmodel_ambient;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientGround;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
uniform highp sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
mediump float t16_2;
highp float t3;
lowp float t10_3;
highp float t6;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 42
    //SAMPLE
    t0.x = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    //Instruction 43
    //MAD
    t3 = _ZBufferParams.x * t0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 44
    //DIV
    t3 = float(1.0) / t3;
    //Instruction 45
    //ADD
    t6 = (-t3) + t0.x;
    //Instruction 46
    //MAD
    t3 = unity_OrthoParams.w * t6 + t3;
    //Instruction 47
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 48
    //ADD
    t6 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 49
    //MAD
    t1.z = t0.x * t6 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 50
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * vec3(t3) + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 51
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = vec3(t3) * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 52
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 53
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 54
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 55
    //MAD
    t0 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 56
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 57
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 58
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 59
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 60
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t0.www + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 61
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
    //Instruction 62
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 63
    //SQRT
    t0.x = sqrt(t0.x);
    //Instruction 64
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.x * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 65
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(t1.xy,t1.z);
    t10_3 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    //Instruction 66
    //ADD
    t16_2 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 67
    //MAD
    t16_2 = t10_3 * t16_2 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 68
    //ADD
    t0 = t0.xxxx + vec4(t16_2);
    //Instruction 69
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 70
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"
}

void main()
{

    //Instruction 141

    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 142
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 143
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 144
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 145
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;

    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 148

    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 149
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 150

    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 151
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 152
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 153
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = t0.yzw * vec3(1.0, 1.0, -1.0);
    //Instruction 154
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 155
    //RET
    return;
}

uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
uniform  sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform  sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform  sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in  vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in  vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in  vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 t0;
lowp vec4 t10_0;
vec4 t1;
float t2;
lowp float t10_2;
float t4;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 112
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    //Instruction 113
    //MAD
    t2 = _ZBufferParams.x * t10_0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 114
    //DIV
    t2 = float(1.0) / t2;
    //Instruction 115
    //ADD
    t4 = (-t2) + t10_0.x;
    //Instruction 116
    //MAD
    t2 = unity_OrthoParams.w * t4 + t2;
    //Instruction 117
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 118
    //ADD
    t4 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 119
    //MAD
    t1.z = t10_0.x * t4 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 120
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * vec3(t2) + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 121
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = vec3(t2) * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 122
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 123
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 124
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 125
    //MAD
    t0 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 126
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 127
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 128
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 129
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 130
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t0.www + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 131
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
    //Instruction 132
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 133
    //SQRT
    t0.x = sqrt(t0.x);
    //Instruction 134
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.x * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 135
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(t1.xy,t1.z);
    t10_2 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    //Instruction 136
    //ADD
    t4 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 137
    //MAD
    t2 = t10_2 * t4 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 138
    //ADD
    SV_Target0 = t0.xxxx + vec4(t2);
    //Instruction 139
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
}

#ifdef VERTEX
attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;
uniform highp vec4 _ProjectionParams;
uniform highp mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;
uniform highp mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
varying highp vec2 xlv_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec3 xlv_TEXCOORD1;
varying highp vec4 xlv_TEXCOORD2;
void main ()
{
  highp vec4 clipPos_1;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_2;
  tmpvar_2 = (glstate_matrix_mvp * _glesVertex);
  clipPos_1.xzw = tmpvar_2.xzw;
  clipPos_1.y = (tmpvar_2.y * _ProjectionParams.x);

  tmpvar_3.zw = vec2(-1.0, 1.0);
  tmpvar_3.xy = clipPos_1.xy;
  highp vec4 tmpvar_4;
  tmpvar_4 = (unity_CameraInvProjection * tmpvar_3);
  highp vec4 tmpvar_5;
  tmpvar_5.zw = vec2(1.0, 1.0);

  tmpvar_6.xy = tmpvar_4.xy;

  gl_Position = tmpvar_2;

#ifdef FRAGMENT

uniform highp vec4 _LightSplitsFar;

    //Instruction 262

    //MOV

    //Instruction 315
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(t1.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    //Instruction 316
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec4 = vec3(t1.zw,t8.z);
    t10_18 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec4, 0.0);
    //Instruction 317
    //MAD
    t8.x = t5.x * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 318
    //MAD
    t1 = t2.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t4.xyzy;
    //Instruction 319
    //MAD
    t3 = t2.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t4.xwzw;
    //Instruction 320
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec5 = vec3(t1.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec5, 0.0);
    //Instruction 321
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec6 = vec3(t1.zw,t8.z);
    t10_2 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec6, 0.0);
    //Instruction 322
    //MAD
    t8.x = t10_16 * 49.000000 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 323
    //MAD
    t8.x = t5.y * t10_2 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 324
    //MAD
    t8.x = t7.x * t10_18 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 325
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec7 = vec3(t3.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec7, 0.0);
    //Instruction 326
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec8 = vec3(t3.zw,t8.z);
    t10_24 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec8, 0.0);
    //Instruction 327
    //MAD
    t8.x = t7.y * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 328
    //MAD
    t8.x = t7.z * t10_24 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 329
    //MUL
    t8.x = t8.x * 0.006944;
    //Instruction 330
    //ADD
    t16_16 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 331
    //MAD
    t8.x = t8.x * t16_16 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 332
    //ADD
    t0 = t0.xxxx + t8.xxxx;
    //Instruction 333
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 334
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"
}

in  vec4 in_POSITION0;

in  vec3 in_NORMAL0;
out vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
vec4 t0;
vec3 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 256
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 257
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 258
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 259
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 260
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 261
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 262
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 263
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 264
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 265
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 266
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 267
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 268
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 269
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = t0.yzw * vec3(1.0, 1.0, -1.0);
    //Instruction 270
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 271
    //RET
    return;
}

uniform  sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;

uniform  sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in  vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in  vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in  vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 t0;
lowp vec4 t10_0;
vec4 t1;
lowp float t10_1;
bvec4 tb1;
vec4 t2;
bvec4 tb2;
vec4 t3;
vec4 t4;
vec3 t5;
vec4 t6;
vec3 t7;
vec3 t8;
lowp float t10_8;
float t16;
lowp float t10_16;
vec2 t17;
lowp float t10_17;
lowp float t10_24;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 156
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    //Instruction 157
    //MAD
    t8.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t10_0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 158
    //DIV
    t8.x = float(1.0) / t8.x;
    //Instruction 159
    //ADD
    t16 = (-t8.x) + t10_0.x;
    //Instruction 160
    //MAD
    t8.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 161
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 162
    //ADD
    t16 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 163
    //MAD
    t1.z = t10_0.x * t16 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 164
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t8.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 165
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t8.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 166
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 167
    //GE
    tb1 = greaterThanEqual(t0.zzzz, _LightSplitsNear);
    //Instruction 168
    //AND
    t1 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb1);
    //Instruction 169
    //LT
    tb2 = lessThan(t0.zzzz, _LightSplitsFar);
    //Instruction 170
    //AND
    t2 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb2);
    //Instruction 171
    //MUL
    t1 = t1 * t2;
    //Instruction 172
    //MUL
    t2 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 173
    //MAD
    t2 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t2;
    //Instruction 174
    //MAD
    t2 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t2;
    //Instruction 175
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.z * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 176
    //ADD
    t2 = t2 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 177
    //MUL
    t8.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[1][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 178
    //MAD
    t8.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t8.xyz;
    //Instruction 179
    //MAD
    t8.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t8.xyz;
    //Instruction 180
    //MAD
    t8.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][3].xyz * t2.www + t8.xyz;
    //Instruction 181
    //MUL
    t8.xyz = t1.yyy * t8.xyz;
    //Instruction 182
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 183
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 184
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 185
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t2.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 186
    //MAD
    t8.xyz = t3.xyz * t1.xxx + t8.xyz;
    //Instruction 187
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[2][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 188
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 189
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 190
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][3].xyz * t2.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 191
    //MAD
    t8.xyz = t3.xyz * t1.zzz + t8.xyz;
    //Instruction 192
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t2.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[3][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 193
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][0].xyz * t2.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 194
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][2].xyz * t2.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 195
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][3].xyz * t2.www + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 196
    //MAD
    t8.xyz = t1.xyz * t1.www + t8.xyz;
    //Instruction 197
    //MAD
    t8.xy = t8.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.zw + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 198
    //ROUND_NI
    t1.xy = floor(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 199
    //FRC
    t8.xy = fract(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 200
    //ADD
    t1.xy = t1.xy + vec2(-0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 201
    //MAD
    t17.xy = (-t8.xy) * vec2(2.000000, 2.000000) + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 202
    //MAD
    t2.xy = (-t8.xy) * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(4.000000, 4.000000);
    //Instruction 203
    //DIV
    t17.xy = t17.xy / t2.xy;
    //Instruction 204
    //ADD
    t3.xy = t17.xy + vec2(-2.000000, -2.000000);
    //Instruction 205
    //MOV
    t4.z = t3.y;
    //Instruction 206
    //MAD
    t17.xy = t8.xy * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(1.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 207
    //DIV
    t2.xz = t8.xy / t17.xy;
    //Instruction 208
    //ADD
    t4.xw = t2.xz + vec2(2.000000, 2.000000);
    //Instruction 209
    //MOV
    t3.w = t4.x;
    //Instruction 210
    //ADD
    t2.xz = t8.xy + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 211
    //MUL
    t8.x = t8.x * 3.000000;
    //Instruction 212
    //MAD
    t5.xz = t8.xx * vec2(-1.0, 1.0) + vec2(4.000000, 1.0);
    //Instruction 213
    //MUL
    t4.xy = t2.xz * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy;
    //Instruction 214
    //MOV
    t6.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.yy;
    //Instruction 215
    //MOV
    t6.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 216
    //MUL
    t6.xyz = t4.zyw * t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 217
    //MOV
    t3.z = t4.x;
    //Instruction 218
    //MOV
    t4.w = t6.x;
    //Instruction 219
    //MOV
    t7.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xx;
    //Instruction 220
    //MOV
    t7.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 221
    //MUL
    t4.xyz = t3.zxw * t7.yxz;
    //Instruction 222
    //MAD
    t3 = t1.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t4.ywxw;
    //Instruction 223
    //MAD
    t8.xy = t1.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy + t4.zw;
    //Instruction 224
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(t8.xy,t8.z);
    t10_8 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    //Instruction 225
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(t3.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    //Instruction 226
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec4 = vec3(t3.zw,t8.z);
    t10_17 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec4, 0.0);
    //Instruction 227
    //MOV
    t5.y = 7.000000;
    //Instruction 228
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t2.yyy * t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 229
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t17.yyy * t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 230
    //MUL
    t5.xy = t5.xz * vec2(7.000000, 7.000000);
    //Instruction 231
    //MUL
    t17.x = t10_17 * t2.y;
    //Instruction 232
    //MAD
    t16 = t2.x * t10_16 + t17.x;
    //Instruction 233
    //MAD
    t8.x = t2.z * t10_8 + t16;
    //Instruction 234
    //MOV
    t6.w = t4.y;
    //Instruction 235
    //MAD
    t2 = t1.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t6.wywz;
    //Instruction 236
    //MOV
    t4.yw = t6.yz;
    //Instruction 237
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec5 = vec3(t2.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec5, 0.0);
    //Instruction 238
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec6 = vec3(t2.zw,t8.z);
    t10_17 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec6, 0.0);
    //Instruction 239
    //MAD
    t8.x = t5.x * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 240
    //MAD
    t2 = t1.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t4.xyzy;
    //Instruction 241
    //MAD
    t4 = t1.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t4.xwzw;
    //Instruction 242
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec7 = vec3(t2.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec7, 0.0);
    //Instruction 243
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec8 = vec3(t2.zw,t8.z);
    t10_1 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec8, 0.0);
    //Instruction 244
    //MAD
    t8.x = t10_16 * 49.000000 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 245
    //MAD
    t8.x = t5.y * t10_1 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 246
    //MAD
    t8.x = t3.x * t10_17 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 247
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec9 = vec3(t4.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec9, 0.0);
    //Instruction 248
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec10 = vec3(t4.zw,t8.z);
    t10_24 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec10, 0.0);
    //Instruction 249
    //MAD
    t8.x = t3.y * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 250
    //MAD
    t8.x = t3.z * t10_24 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 251
    //MUL
    t8.x = t8.x * 0.006944;
    //Instruction 252
    //ADD
    t16 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 253
    //MAD
    t8.x = t8.x * t16 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 254
    //ADD
    SV_Target0 = t0.xxxx + t8.xxxx;
    //Instruction 255
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif

SubProgram "gles " {
Keywords { "SHADOWS_SPLIT_SPHERES" "SHADOWS_NONATIVE" }
"!!GLES
#version 100

#ifdef VERTEX
attribute vec4 _glesVertex;
attribute vec3 _glesNormal;
attribute vec4 _glesMultiTexCoord0;

SubProgram "gles3 " {
Keywords { "SHADOWS_SPLIT_SPHERES" "SHADOWS_NATIVE" }
"!!GLES3
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 300 es
precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
uniform 	vec4 _SinTime;
uniform 	vec4 _CosTime;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DeltaTime;

uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;

uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec3 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 384
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 385
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 386
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 387
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 388
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 389
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 390
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 391
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 392
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 393
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 394
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 395
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 396
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 397
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = vec3(t0.y * float(1.0), t0.z * float(1.0), t0.w * float(-1.0));
    //Instruction 398
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 399
    //RET
    return;
}
