uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
uniform highp sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
lowp float t10_1;
bvec4 tb1;
highp vec4 t2;
highp vec4 t3;
lowp vec3 t10_3;
highp vec4 t4;
highp vec3 t5;
highp vec4 t6;
highp vec3 t7;
highp vec3 t8;
lowp float t10_8;
highp vec3 t9;
highp float t16;
mediump float t16_16;
lowp float t10_16;
highp vec2 t17;
lowp float t10_17;
lowp float t10_24;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 272
    //SAMPLE
    t0.x = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    //Instruction 273
    //MAD
    t8.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 274
    //DIV
    t8.x = float(1.0) / t8.x;
    //Instruction 275
    //ADD
    t16 = (-t8.x) + t0.x;
    //Instruction 276
    //MAD
    t8.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 277
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 278
    //ADD
    t16 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 279
    //MAD
    t1.z = t0.x * t16 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 280
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t8.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 281
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t8.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 282
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 283
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 284
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 285
    //MAD
    t0 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 286
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 287
    //ADD
    t1.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[0].xyz);
    //Instruction 288
    //DP3
    t1.x = dot(t1.xyz, t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 289
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[1].xyz);
    //Instruction 290
    //DP3
    t1.y = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 291
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 292
    //DP3
    t1.z = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 293
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[3].xyz);
    //Instruction 294
    //DP3
    t1.w = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 295
    //LT
    tb1 = lessThan(t1, unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii);
    //Instruction 296
    //MOVC
    t10_3.x = (tb1.x) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    t10_3.y = (tb1.y) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    t10_3.z = (tb1.z) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    //Instruction 297
    //AND
    t1 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb1);
    //Instruction 298
    //ADD
    t10_3.xyz = vec3(t10_3.x + t1.y, t10_3.y + t1.z, t10_3.z + t1.w);
    //Instruction 299
    //MAX
    t10_3.xyz = max(t10_3.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    //Instruction 300
    //MUL
    t9.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[1][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 301
    //MAD
    t9.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t9.xyz;
    //Instruction 302
    //MAD
    t9.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t9.xyz;
    //Instruction 303
    //MAD
    t9.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][3].xyz * t0.www + t9.xyz;
    //Instruction 304
    //MUL
    t9.xyz = t10_3.xxx * t9.xyz;
    //Instruction 305
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 306
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 307
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 308
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 309
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = t2.xyz * t1.xxx + t9.xyz;
    //Instruction 310
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[2][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 311
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 312
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 313
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 314
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = t2.xyz * t10_3.yyy + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 315
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[3][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 316
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 317
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 318
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 319
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
    //Instruction 320
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 321
    //SQRT
    t0.x = sqrt(t0.x);
    //Instruction 322
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.x * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 323
    //MAD
    t8.xyz = t2.xyz * t10_3.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 324
    //MAD
    t8.xy = t8.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.zw + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 325
    //ROUND_NI
    t1.xy = floor(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 326
    //FRC
    t8.xy = fract(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 327
    //ADD
    t1.xy = t1.xy + vec2(-0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 328
    //MAD
    t17.xy = (-t8.xy) * vec2(2.000000, 2.000000) + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 329
    //MAD
    t2.xy = (-t8.xy) * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(4.000000, 4.000000);
    //Instruction 330
    //DIV
    t17.xy = t17.xy / t2.xy;
    //Instruction 331
    //ADD
    t3.xy = t17.xy + vec2(-2.000000, -2.000000);
    //Instruction 332
    //MOV
    t4.z = t3.y;
    //Instruction 333
    //MAD
    t17.xy = t8.xy * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(1.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 334
    //DIV
    t2.xz = t8.xy / t17.xy;
    //Instruction 335
    //ADD
    t4.xw = t2.xz + vec2(2.000000, 2.000000);
    //Instruction 336
    //MOV
    t3.w = t4.x;
    //Instruction 337
    //ADD
    t2.xz = t8.xy + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 338
    //MUL
    t8.x = t8.x * 3.000000;
    //Instruction 339
    //MAD
    t5.xz = t8.xx * vec2(-1.0, 1.0) + vec2(4.000000, 1.0);
    //Instruction 340
    //MUL
    t4.xy = t2.xz * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy;
    //Instruction 341
    //MOV
    t6.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.yy;
    //Instruction 342
    //MOV
    t6.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 343
    //MUL
    t6.xyz = vec3(t4.z * t6.x, t4.y * t6.y, t4.w * t6.z);
    //Instruction 344
    //MOV
    t3.z = t4.x;
    //Instruction 345
    //MOV
    t4.w = t6.x;
    //Instruction 346
    //MOV
    t7.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xx;
    //Instruction 347
    //MOV
    t7.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 348
    //MUL
    t4.xyz = t3.zxw * t7.yxz;
    //Instruction 349
    //MAD
    t3 = t1.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t4.ywxw;
    //Instruction 350
    //MAD
    t8.xy = t1.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy + t4.zw;
    //Instruction 351
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec11 = vec3(t8.xy,t8.z);
    t10_8 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec11, 0.0);
    //Instruction 352
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec12 = vec3(t3.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec12, 0.0);
    //Instruction 353
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec13 = vec3(t3.zw,t8.z);
    t10_17 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec13, 0.0);
    //Instruction 354
    //MOV
    t5.y = 7.000000;
    //Instruction 355
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t2.yyy * t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 356
    //MUL
    t7.xyz = t17.yyy * t5.xyz;
    //Instruction 357
    //MUL
    t5.xy = t5.xz * vec2(7.000000, 7.000000);
    //Instruction 358
    //MUL
    t17.x = t10_17 * t2.y;
    //Instruction 359
    //MAD
    t16 = t2.x * t10_16 + t17.x;
    //Instruction 360
    //MAD
    t8.x = t2.z * t10_8 + t16;
    //Instruction 361
    //MOV
    t6.w = t4.y;
    //Instruction 362
    //MAD
    t2 = t1.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t6.wywz;
    //Instruction 363
    //MOV
    t4.yw = t6.yz;
    //Instruction 364
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec14 = vec3(t2.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec14, 0.0);
    //Instruction 365
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec15 = vec3(t2.zw,t8.z);
    t10_17 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec15, 0.0);
    //Instruction 366
    //MAD
    t8.x = t5.x * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 367
    //MAD
    t2 = t1.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t4.xyzy;
    //Instruction 368
    //MAD
    t3 = t1.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t4.xwzw;
    //Instruction 369
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec16 = vec3(t2.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec16, 0.0);
    //Instruction 370
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec17 = vec3(t2.zw,t8.z);
    t10_1 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec17, 0.0);
    //Instruction 371
    //MAD
    t8.x = t10_16 * 49.000000 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 372
    //MAD
    t8.x = t5.y * t10_1 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 373
    //MAD
    t8.x = t7.x * t10_17 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 374
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec18 = vec3(t3.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec18, 0.0);
    //Instruction 375
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec19 = vec3(t3.zw,t8.z);
    t10_24 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec19, 0.0);
    //Instruction 376
    //MAD
    t8.x = t7.y * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 377
    //MAD
    t8.x = t7.z * t10_24 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 378
    //MUL
    t8.x = t8.x * 0.006944;
    //Instruction 379
    //ADD
    t16_16 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 380
    //MAD
    t8.x = t8.x * t16_16 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 381
    //ADD
    t0 = t0.xxxx + t8.xxxx;
    //Instruction 382
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 383
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
SubProgram "glcore " {
Keywords { "SHADOWS_SPLIT_SPHERES" "SHADOWS_NATIVE" }
"!!GL2x
#ifdef VERTEX

uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
in  vec4 in_POSITION0;
in  vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in  vec3 in_NORMAL0;
out vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
vec4 t0;
vec3 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 288
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 289
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 290
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 291
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 292
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 293
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 294
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 295
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 296
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 297
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 298
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 299
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 300
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 301
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = t0.yzw * vec3(1.0, 1.0, -1.0);
    //Instruction 302
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 303
    //RET
    return;
}

#extension GL_ARB_shader_bit_encoding : require
uniform 	vec4 _Time;

uniform 	vec4 unity_AmbientSky;

uniform  sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform  sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in  vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in  vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in  vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 t0;
lowp vec4 t10_0;
vec4 t1;
lowp float t10_1;
bvec4 tb1;
vec4 t2;
vec4 t3;
vec4 t4;
vec3 t5;
vec4 t6;
vec3 t7;

lowp float t10_8;

void main()
{
    //Instruction 177
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    //Instruction 178
    //MAD
    t8.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t10_0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 179
    //DIV
    t8.x = float(1.0) / t8.x;
    //Instruction 180
    //ADD
    t16 = (-t8.x) + t10_0.x;
    //Instruction 181
    //MAD
    t8.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 182
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 183
    //ADD
    t16 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 184
    //MAD
    t1.z = t10_0.x * t16 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 185
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t8.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 186
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t8.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 187
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 188
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 189
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 190
    //MAD
    t0 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 191
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 192
    //ADD
    t1.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[0].xyz);
    //Instruction 193
    //DP3
    t1.x = dot(t1.xyz, t1.xyz);
    //Instruction 194
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[1].xyz);
    //Instruction 195
    //DP3
    t1.y = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 196
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 197
    //DP3
    t1.z = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 198
    //ADD
    t2.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[3].xyz);
    //Instruction 199
    //DP3
    t1.w = dot(t2.xyz, t2.xyz);
    //Instruction 200
    //LT
    tb1 = lessThan(t1, unity_ShadowSplitSqRadii);
    //Instruction 201
    //MOVC
    t2.x = (tb1.x) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    t2.y = (tb1.y) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    t2.z = (tb1.z) ? float(-1.0) : float(-0.000000);
    //Instruction 202
    //AND
    t1 = mix(vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0), vec4(1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0), tb1);
    //Instruction 203
    //ADD
    t9.xyz = t2.xyz + t1.yzw;
    //Instruction 204
    //MAX
    t9.xyz = max(t9.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    //Instruction 205
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[1][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 206
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 207
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 208
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[1][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 209
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t9.xxx * t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 210
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 211
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 212
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 213
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t0.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 214
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = t3.xyz * t1.xxx + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 215
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[2][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 216
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 217
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 218
    //MAD
    t3.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[2][3].xyz * t0.www + t3.xyz;
    //Instruction 219
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = t3.xyz * t9.yyy + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 220

    t2.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[3][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 221
    //MAD

    //Instruction 222
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 223
    //MAD
    t2.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[3][3].xyz * t0.www + t2.xyz;
    //Instruction 224
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
    //Instruction 225
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 226
    //SQRT
    t0.x = sqrt(t0.x);
    //Instruction 227
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.x * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 228
    //MAD

    //Instruction 229
    //MAD
    t8.xy = t8.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.zw + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 230
    //ROUND_NI
    t1.xy = floor(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 231
    //FRC
    t8.xy = fract(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 232
    //ADD
    t1.xy = t1.xy + vec2(-0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 233
    //MAD

    //DIV
    t17.xy = t17.xy / t2.xy;
    //Instruction 236

    t2.xz = t8.xy / t17.xy;

    //ADD
    t4.xw = t2.xz + vec2(2.000000, 2.000000);
    //Instruction 241
    //MOV
    t3.w = t4.x;

    //ADD

    //Instruction 243

    //Instruction 245
    //MUL

    //Instruction 246
    //MOV

    //Instruction 247
    //MOV
    t6.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 248
    //MUL

    //Instruction 249
    //MOV

    //Instruction 250

    //MOV

    //MAD

    //Instruction 256
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ

    //Instruction 261

    //MAD

    //Instruction 265
    //MAD
    t8.x = t2.z * t10_8 + t16;
    //Instruction 266
    //MOV

    //Instruction 272
    //MAD

    //Instruction 273

    t10_1 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec6, 0.0);
    //Instruction 276
    //MAD
    t8.x = t10_16 * 49.000000 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 277
    //MAD
    t8.x = t5.y * t10_1 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 278

    //Instruction 279
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec7 = vec3(t4.xy,t8.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec7, 0.0);

    //SAMPLE_C_LZ

    //Instruction 282

    t16 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 285

    //Instruction 286

    SV_Target0 = t0.xxxx + t8.xxxx;

uniform 	vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;
uniform 	vec4 _LightPositionRange;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosX0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosY0;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosZ0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_4LightAtten0;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightColor[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightPosition[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_LightAtten[8];
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpotDirection[8];
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;

uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;

uniform 	vec4 _LightSplitsFar;
uniform 	mat4 unity_World2Shadow[4];
uniform 	mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;
uniform 	mat4 _World2Object;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_transpose_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;
uniform 	lowp vec4 glstate_lightmodel_ambient;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientGround;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec3 t1;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 205
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 206
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 207
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 208
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 209
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 210
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 211
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 212
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 213
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 214
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 215
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 216
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 217
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 218
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = vec3(t0.y * float(1.0), t0.z * float(1.0), t0.w * float(-1.0));
    //Instruction 219
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 220
    //RET
    return;
}

#version 300 es
precision highp float;
uniform 	vec4 _Time;

uniform 	vec4 _ProjectionParams;

uniform 	vec4 unity_OrthoParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_CameraWorldClipPlanes[6];
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraProjection;
uniform 	mat4 unity_CameraInvProjection;
uniform 	vec4 _WorldSpaceLightPos0;
uniform 	vec4 _LightPositionRange;
uniform 	vec4 unity_4LightPosX0;

uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowSplitSpheres[4];

uniform 	mediump vec4 _LightShadowData;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_mvp;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_invtrans_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 _Object2World;
uniform 	mat4 _World2Object;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LODFade;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_transpose_modelview0;
uniform 	mat4 glstate_matrix_projection;
uniform 	lowp vec4 glstate_lightmodel_ambient;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixV;
uniform 	mat4 unity_MatrixVP;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientSky;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientEquator;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_AmbientGround;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_FogColor;
uniform 	vec4 unity_FogParams;
uniform 	vec4 unity_LightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_DynamicLightmapST;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube0_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube0_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMax;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_BoxMin;
uniform 	vec4 unity_SpecCube1_ProbePosition;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_SpecCube1_HDR;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceGrey;
uniform 	lowp vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDouble;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceDielectricSpec;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_ColorSpaceLuminance;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_Lightmap_HDR;
uniform 	mediump vec4 unity_DynamicLightmap_HDR;
uniform 	vec4 unity_ShadowCascadeScales;
uniform 	mat4 _CameraToWorld;
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize;
uniform highp sampler2D _CameraDepthTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture;
uniform lowp sampler2D _ShadowMapTexture;
in highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
layout(location = 0) out lowp vec4 SV_Target0;
highp vec4 t0;
highp vec4 t1;
lowp float t10_1;
highp vec3 t2;
lowp float t10_2;
highp vec4 t3;
highp vec4 t4;
highp vec4 t5;
highp vec3 t6;
highp vec3 t7;
lowp float t10_7;
lowp float t10_8;
highp vec2 t9;
lowp float t10_9;
highp float t14;
mediump float t16_14;
lowp float t10_14;
lowp float t10_15;
highp vec2 t16;
lowp float t10_21;
highp float t22;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 125
    //SAMPLE
    t0.x = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    //Instruction 126
    //MAD
    t7.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 127
    //DIV
    t7.x = float(1.0) / t7.x;
    //Instruction 128
    //ADD
    t14 = (-t7.x) + t0.x;
    //Instruction 129
    //MAD
    t7.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t14 + t7.x;
    //Instruction 130
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 131
    //ADD
    t14 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 132
    //MAD
    t1.z = t0.x * t14 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 133
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t7.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 134
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t7.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 135
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 136
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 137
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 138
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 139
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.z * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 140
    //ADD
    t1 = t1 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 141
    //MUL
    t7.xyz = t1.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 142
    //MAD
    t7.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t1.xxx + t7.xyz;
    //Instruction 143
    //MAD
    t7.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t1.zzz + t7.xyz;
    //Instruction 144
    //MAD
    t7.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t1.www + t7.xyz;
    //Instruction 145
    //MOV
    t1.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.yy;
    //Instruction 146
    //MOV
    t1.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 147
    //MAD
    t7.xy = t7.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.zw + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 148
    //FRC
    t2.xy = fract(t7.xy);
    //Instruction 149
    //ROUND_NI
    t7.xy = floor(t7.xy);
    //Instruction 150
    //ADD
    t7.xy = t7.xy + vec2(-0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 151
    //MAD
    t16.xy = (-t2.xy) * vec2(2.000000, 2.000000) + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 152
    //MAD
    t3.xy = (-t2.xy) * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(4.000000, 4.000000);
    //Instruction 153
    //DIV
    t16.xy = t16.xy / t3.xy;
    //Instruction 154
    //ADD
    t4.xy = t16.xy + vec2(-2.000000, -2.000000);
    //Instruction 155
    //MOV
    t5.z = t4.y;
    //Instruction 156
    //MAD
    t16.xy = t2.xy * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(1.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 157
    //DIV
    t3.xz = t2.xy / t16.xy;
    //Instruction 158
    //ADD
    t5.xw = t3.xz + vec2(2.000000, 2.000000);
    //Instruction 159
    //MOV
    t4.w = t5.x;
    //Instruction 160
    //ADD
    t9.xy = t2.xy + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 161
    //MUL
    t22 = t2.x * 3.000000;
    //Instruction 162
    //MAD
    t6.xz = vec2(t22) * vec2(-1.0, 1.0) + vec2(4.000000, 1.0);
    //Instruction 163
    //MUL
    t5.xy = t9.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy;
    //Instruction 164
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = vec3(t1.x * t5.z, t1.y * t5.y, t1.z * t5.w);
    //Instruction 165
    //MOV
    t4.z = t5.x;
    //Instruction 166
    //MOV
    t5.w = t1.x;
    //Instruction 167
    //MOV
    t2.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xx;
    //Instruction 168
    //MOV
    t2.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 169
    //MUL
    t5.xyz = t2.yxz * t4.zxw;
    //Instruction 170
    //MAD
    t4 = t7.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t5.ywxw;
    //Instruction 171
    //MAD
    t2.xy = t7.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy + t5.zw;
    //Instruction 172
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(t2.xy,t7.z);
    t10_1 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    //Instruction 173
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(t4.xy,t7.z);
    t10_2 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    //Instruction 174
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(t4.zw,t7.z);
    t10_9 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    //Instruction 175
    //MOV
    t6.y = 7.000000;
    //Instruction 176
    //MUL
    t3.xyz = t3.yyy * t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 177
    //MUL
    t4.xyz = t16.yyy * t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 178
    //MUL
    t16.xy = t6.xz * vec2(7.000000, 7.000000);
    //Instruction 179
    //MUL
    t9.x = t10_9 * t3.y;
    //Instruction 180
    //MAD
    t2.x = t3.x * t10_2 + t9.x;
    //Instruction 181
    //MAD
    t1.x = t3.z * t10_1 + t2.x;
    //Instruction 182
    //MOV
    t1.w = t5.y;
    //Instruction 183
    //MAD
    t3 = t7.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t1.wywz;
    //Instruction 184
    //MOV
    t5.yw = t1.yz;
    //Instruction 185
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec4 = vec3(t3.xy,t7.z);
    t10_8 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec4, 0.0);
    //Instruction 186
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec5 = vec3(t3.zw,t7.z);
    t10_15 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec5, 0.0);
    //Instruction 187
    //MAD
    t1.x = t16.x * t10_8 + t1.x;
    //Instruction 188
    //MAD
    t3 = t7.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t5.xyzy;
    //Instruction 189
    //MAD
    t5 = t7.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t5.xwzw;
    //Instruction 190
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec6 = vec3(t3.xy,t7.z);
    t10_7 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec6, 0.0);
    //Instruction 191
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec7 = vec3(t3.zw,t7.z);
    t10_14 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec7, 0.0);
    //Instruction 192
    //MAD
    t7.x = t10_7 * 49.000000 + t1.x;
    //Instruction 193
    //MAD
    t7.x = t16.y * t10_14 + t7.x;
    //Instruction 194
    //MAD
    t7.x = t4.x * t10_15 + t7.x;
    //Instruction 195
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec8 = vec3(t5.xy,t7.z);
    t10_14 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec8, 0.0);
    //Instruction 196
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec9 = vec3(t5.zw,t7.z);
    t10_21 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec9, 0.0);
    //Instruction 197
    //MAD
    t7.x = t4.y * t10_14 + t7.x;
    //Instruction 198
    //MAD
    t7.x = t4.z * t10_21 + t7.x;
    //Instruction 199
    //MUL
    t7.x = t7.x * 0.006944;
    //Instruction 200
    //ADD
    t16_14 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 201
    //MAD
    t7.x = t7.x * t16_14 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 202
    //ADD
    t0 = t0.xxxx + t7.xxxx;
    //Instruction 203
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 204
    //RET
    return;
}

  shadow_10 = tmpvar_66;
  highp float tmpvar_67;
  highp vec3 tmpvar_68;
  tmpvar_68 = (tmpvar_6.xyz - unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
  mediump float tmpvar_69;
  highp float tmpvar_70;
  tmpvar_70 = clamp (((
    sqrt(dot (tmpvar_68, tmpvar_68))
   * _LightShadowData.z) + _LightShadowData.w), 0.0, 1.0);
  tmpvar_69 = tmpvar_70;
  tmpvar_67 = tmpvar_69;
  shadow_2 = (tmpvar_66 + tmpvar_67);
  mediump vec4 tmpvar_71;
  tmpvar_71 = vec4(shadow_2);
  tmpvar_1 = tmpvar_71;
  gl_FragData[0] = tmpvar_1;
}


#endif
"
}

    //MOV

    //Instruction 437
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 438
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 439
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 440
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 441
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 442
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 443
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 444
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 445
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 446
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 447
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = vec3(t0.y * float(1.0), t0.z * float(1.0), t0.w * float(-1.0));
    //Instruction 448
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 449
    //RET
    return;

highp vec3 t9;
lowp float t10_9;
highp float t16;
mediump float t16_16;
lowp float t10_16;
highp vec2 t19;
highp float t24;
lowp float t10_24;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 351
    //SAMPLE
    t0.x = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).x;
    //Instruction 352
    //MAD
    t8.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 353
    //DIV
    t8.x = float(1.0) / t8.x;
    //Instruction 354
    //ADD
    t16 = (-t8.x) + t0.x;
    //Instruction 355
    //MAD
    t8.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 356
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 357
    //ADD
    t16 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 358
    //MAD
    t1.z = t0.x * t16 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 359
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t8.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 360
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t8.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 361
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 362
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 363
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 364
    //MAD
    t0 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 365
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 366
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 367
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 368
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 369
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t0.www + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 370
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
    //Instruction 371
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 372
    //SQRT
    t0.x = sqrt(t0.x);
    //Instruction 373
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.x * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 374
    //MOV
    t2.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.yy;
    //Instruction 375
    //MOV
    t2.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 376
    //MAD
    t8.xy = t1.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.zw + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 377
    //FRC
    t1.xy = fract(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 378
    //ROUND_NI
    t8.xy = floor(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 379
    //ADD
    t8.xy = t8.xy + vec2(-0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 380
    //MAD
    t3.xy = (-t1.xy) * vec2(2.000000, 2.000000) + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 381
    //MAD
    t19.xy = (-t1.xy) * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(4.000000, 4.000000);
    //Instruction 382
    //DIV
    t3.xy = t3.xy / t19.xy;
    //Instruction 383
    //ADD
    t4.xy = t3.xy + vec2(-2.000000, -2.000000);
    //Instruction 384
    //MOV
    t5.z = t4.y;
    //Instruction 385
    //MAD
    t3.xy = t1.xy * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(1.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 386
    //DIV
    t3.xz = t1.xy / t3.xy;
    //Instruction 387
    //ADD
    t5.xw = t3.xz + vec2(2.000000, 2.000000);
    //Instruction 388
    //MOV
    t4.w = t5.x;
    //Instruction 389
    //ADD
    t9.xz = t1.xy + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 390
    //MUL
    t24 = t1.x * 3.000000;
    //Instruction 391
    //MAD
    t6.xz = vec2(t24) * vec2(-1.0, 1.0) + vec2(4.000000, 1.0);
    //Instruction 392
    //MUL
    t5.xy = t9.xz * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy;
    //Instruction 393
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = vec3(t2.x * t5.z, t2.y * t5.y, t2.z * t5.w);
    //Instruction 394
    //MOV
    t4.z = t5.x;
    //Instruction 395
    //MOV
    t5.w = t2.x;
    //Instruction 396
    //MOV
    t7.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xx;
    //Instruction 397
    //MOV
    t7.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 398
    //MUL
    t5.xyz = t4.zxw * t7.yxz;
    //Instruction 399
    //MAD
    t4 = t8.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t5.ywxw;
    //Instruction 400
    //MAD
    t1.xy = t8.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy + t5.zw;
    //Instruction 401
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec9 = vec3(t1.xy,t1.z);
    t10_24 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec9, 0.0);
    //Instruction 402
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec10 = vec3(t4.xy,t1.z);
    t10_1 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec10, 0.0);
    //Instruction 403
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec11 = vec3(t4.zw,t1.z);
    t10_9 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec11, 0.0);
    //Instruction 404
    //MOV
    t6.y = 7.000000;
    //Instruction 405
    //MUL
    t3.xzw = t19.yyy * t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 406
    //MUL
    t4.xyz = t3.yyy * t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 407
    //MUL
    t6.xy = t6.xz * vec2(7.000000, 7.000000);
    //Instruction 408
    //MUL
    t9.x = t10_9 * t3.z;
    //Instruction 409
    //MAD
    t1.x = t3.x * t10_1 + t9.x;
    //Instruction 410
    //MAD
    t24 = t3.w * t10_24 + t1.x;
    //Instruction 411
    //MOV
    t2.w = t5.y;
    //Instruction 412
    //MAD
    t3 = t8.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t2.wywz;
    //Instruction 413
    //MOV
    t5.yw = t2.yz;
    //Instruction 414
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec12 = vec3(t3.xy,t1.z);
    t10_1 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec12, 0.0);
    //Instruction 415
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec13 = vec3(t3.zw,t1.z);
    t10_9 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec13, 0.0);
    //Instruction 416
    //MAD
    t24 = t6.x * t10_1 + t24;
    //Instruction 417
    //MAD
    t2 = t8.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t5.xyzy;
    //Instruction 418
    //MAD
    t3 = t8.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t5.xwzw;
    //Instruction 419
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec14 = vec3(t2.xy,t1.z);
    t10_8 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec14, 0.0);
    //Instruction 420
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec15 = vec3(t2.zw,t1.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec15, 0.0);
    //Instruction 421
    //MAD
    t8.x = t10_8 * 49.000000 + t24;
    //Instruction 422
    //MAD
    t8.x = t6.y * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 423
    //MAD
    t8.x = t4.x * t10_9 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 424
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec16 = vec3(t3.xy,t1.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec16, 0.0);
    //Instruction 425
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec17 = vec3(t3.zw,t1.z);
    t10_24 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec17, 0.0);
    //Instruction 426
    //MAD
    t8.x = t4.y * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 427
    //MAD
    t8.x = t4.z * t10_24 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 428
    //MUL
    t8.x = t8.x * 0.006944;
    //Instruction 429
    //ADD
    t16_16 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 430
    //MAD
    t8.x = t8.x * t16_16 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 431
    //ADD
    t0 = t0.xxxx + t8.xxxx;
    //Instruction 432
    //MOV
    SV_Target0 = t0;
    //Instruction 433
    //RET
    return;
}

#endif

    //Instruction 482
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    //Instruction 483
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz = in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    //Instruction 484
    //MUL
    t0 = in_POSITION0.yyyy * glstate_matrix_mvp[1];
    //Instruction 485
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[0] * in_POSITION0.xxxx + t0;
    //Instruction 486
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[2] * in_POSITION0.zzzz + t0;
    //Instruction 487
    //MAD
    t0 = glstate_matrix_mvp[3] * in_POSITION0.wwww + t0;
    //Instruction 488
    //MUL
    t1.x = t0.y * _ProjectionParams.x;
    //Instruction 489
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t1.xxx * unity_CameraInvProjection[1].xyz;
    //Instruction 490
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_CameraInvProjection[0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 491
    //MOV
    gl_Position = t0;
    //Instruction 492
    //ADD
    t0.x = t1.z + unity_CameraInvProjection[2].z;
    //Instruction 493
    //ADD
    t0.yzw = t1.xyz + (-unity_CameraInvProjection[2].xyz);
    //Instruction 494
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + unity_CameraInvProjection[3].zxyz;
    //Instruction 495
    //MUL
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = t0.yzw * vec3(1.0, 1.0, -1.0);
    //Instruction 496
    //MOV
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = (-t0.x);
    //Instruction 497
    //RET
    return;
}

vec4 t0;

lowp float t10_24;
void main()
{
    //Instruction 400
    //SAMPLE
    t10_0 = texture(_CameraDepthTexture, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    //Instruction 401
    //MAD
    t8.x = _ZBufferParams.x * t10_0.x + _ZBufferParams.y;
    //Instruction 402
    //DIV
    t8.x = float(1.0) / t8.x;
    //Instruction 403
    //ADD
    t16 = (-t8.x) + t10_0.x;
    //Instruction 404
    //MAD
    t8.x = unity_OrthoParams.w * t16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 405
    //MOV
    t1.xy = vs_TEXCOORD2.xy;
    //Instruction 406
    //ADD
    t16 = (-vs_TEXCOORD2.z) + vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    //Instruction 407
    //MAD
    t1.z = t10_0.x * t16 + vs_TEXCOORD2.z;
    //Instruction 408
    //MAD
    t0.xzw = (-vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz) * t8.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 409
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t8.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz;
    //Instruction 410
    //MAD
    t0.xyz = unity_OrthoParams.www * t0.xzw + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 411
    //MUL
    t1 = t0.yyyy * _CameraToWorld[1];
    //Instruction 412
    //MAD
    t1 = _CameraToWorld[0] * t0.xxxx + t1;
    //Instruction 413
    //MAD
    t0 = _CameraToWorld[2] * t0.zzzz + t1;
    //Instruction 414
    //ADD
    t0 = t0 + _CameraToWorld[3];
    //Instruction 415
    //MUL
    t1.xyz = t0.yyy * unity_World2Shadow[0][1].xyz;
    //Instruction 416
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][0].xyz * t0.xxx + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 417
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][2].xyz * t0.zzz + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 418
    //MAD
    t1.xyz = unity_World2Shadow[0][3].xyz * t0.www + t1.xyz;
    //Instruction 419
    //ADD
    t0.xyz = t0.xyz + (-unity_ShadowFadeCenterAndType.xyz);
    //Instruction 420
    //DP3
    t0.x = dot(t0.xyz, t0.xyz);
    //Instruction 421
    //SQRT
    t0.x = sqrt(t0.x);
    //Instruction 422
    //MAD
    t0.x = t0.x * _LightShadowData.z + _LightShadowData.w;
    t0.x = clamp(t0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 423
    //MOV
    t2.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.yy;
    //Instruction 424
    //MOV
    t2.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 425
    //MAD
    t8.xy = t1.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.zw + vec2(0.500000, 0.500000);
    //Instruction 426
    //FRC
    t1.xy = fract(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 427
    //ROUND_NI
    t8.xy = floor(t8.xy);
    //Instruction 428
    //ADD
    t8.xy = t8.xy + vec2(-0.500000, -0.500000);
    //Instruction 429
    //MAD
    t3.xy = (-t1.xy) * vec2(2.000000, 2.000000) + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 430
    //MAD
    t19.xy = (-t1.xy) * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(4.000000, 4.000000);
    //Instruction 431
    //DIV
    t3.xy = t3.xy / t19.xy;
    //Instruction 432
    //ADD
    t4.xy = t3.xy + vec2(-2.000000, -2.000000);
    //Instruction 433
    //MOV
    t5.z = t4.y;
    //Instruction 434
    //MAD
    t3.xy = t1.xy * vec2(3.000000, 3.000000) + vec2(1.0, 1.0);
    //Instruction 435
    //DIV
    t3.xz = t1.xy / t3.xy;
    //Instruction 436
    //ADD
    t5.xw = t3.xz + vec2(2.000000, 2.000000);
    //Instruction 437
    //MOV
    t4.w = t5.x;
    //Instruction 438
    //ADD
    t9.xz = t1.xy + vec2(3.000000, 3.000000);
    //Instruction 439
    //MUL
    t24 = t1.x * 3.000000;
    //Instruction 440
    //MAD
    t6.xz = vec2(t24) * vec2(-1.0, 1.0) + vec2(4.000000, 1.0);
    //Instruction 441
    //MUL
    t5.xy = t9.xz * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy;
    //Instruction 442
    //MUL
    t2.xyz = t2.xyz * t5.zyw;
    //Instruction 443
    //MOV
    t4.z = t5.x;
    //Instruction 444
    //MOV
    t5.w = t2.x;
    //Instruction 445
    //MOV
    t7.xz = _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xx;
    //Instruction 446
    //MOV
    t7.y = 0.142857;
    //Instruction 447
    //MUL
    t5.xyz = t4.zxw * t7.yxz;
    //Instruction 448
    //MAD
    t4 = t8.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t5.ywxw;
    //Instruction 449
    //MAD
    t1.xy = t8.xy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xy + t5.zw;
    //Instruction 450
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec20 = vec3(t1.xy,t1.z);
    t10_24 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec20, 0.0);
    //Instruction 451
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec21 = vec3(t4.xy,t1.z);
    t10_1 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec21, 0.0);
    //Instruction 452
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec22 = vec3(t4.zw,t1.z);
    t10_9 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec22, 0.0);
    //Instruction 453
    //MOV
    t6.y = 7.000000;
    //Instruction 454
    //MUL
    t3.xzw = t19.yyy * t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 455
    //MUL
    t4.xyz = t3.yyy * t6.xyz;
    //Instruction 456
    //MUL
    t6.xy = t6.xz * vec2(7.000000, 7.000000);
    //Instruction 457
    //MUL
    t9.x = t10_9 * t3.z;
    //Instruction 458
    //MAD
    t1.x = t3.x * t10_1 + t9.x;
    //Instruction 459
    //MAD
    t24 = t3.w * t10_24 + t1.x;
    //Instruction 460
    //MOV
    t2.w = t5.y;
    //Instruction 461
    //MAD
    t3 = t8.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t2.wywz;
    //Instruction 462
    //MOV
    t5.yw = t2.yz;
    //Instruction 463
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec23 = vec3(t3.xy,t1.z);
    t10_1 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec23, 0.0);
    //Instruction 464
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec24 = vec3(t3.zw,t1.z);
    t10_9 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec24, 0.0);
    //Instruction 465
    //MAD
    t24 = t6.x * t10_1 + t24;
    //Instruction 466
    //MAD
    t2 = t8.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t5.xyzy;
    //Instruction 467
    //MAD
    t3 = t8.xyxy * _ShadowMapTexture_TexelSize.xyxy + t5.xwzw;
    //Instruction 468
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec25 = vec3(t2.xy,t1.z);
    t10_8 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec25, 0.0);
    //Instruction 469
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec26 = vec3(t2.zw,t1.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec26, 0.0);
    //Instruction 470
    //MAD
    t8.x = t10_8 * 49.000000 + t24;
    //Instruction 471
    //MAD
    t8.x = t6.y * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 472
    //MAD
    t8.x = t4.x * t10_9 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 473
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec27 = vec3(t3.xy,t1.z);
    t10_16 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec27, 0.0);
    //Instruction 474
    //SAMPLE_C_LZ
    vec3 txVec28 = vec3(t3.zw,t1.z);
    t10_24 = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_ShadowMapTexture, txVec28, 0.0);
    //Instruction 475
    //MAD
    t8.x = t4.y * t10_16 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 476
    //MAD
    t8.x = t4.z * t10_24 + t8.x;
    //Instruction 477
    //MUL
    t8.x = t8.x * 0.006944;
    //Instruction 478
    //ADD
    t16 = (-_LightShadowData.x) + 1.0;
    //Instruction 479
    //MAD
    t8.x = t8.x * t16 + _LightShadowData.x;
    //Instruction 480
    //ADD
    SV_Target0 = t0.xxxx + t8.xxxx;
    //Instruction 481
    //RET
    return;
